<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c78ac5f3-ee60-4735-a6a5-285d12e14a6f'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer596334316617561348">Left alone in Baltimore after his unpredictable lover bails, Special Agent Zane Garrett takes his frustration out on everything in his path until he is ordered to Chicago to back up an undercover operative. When he gets there, though, he finds himself face to face with his wayward partner, Special Agent Ty Grady. They have to deal with the uncertainty lingering between the</span>
  <span id="freeText596334316617561348" style="display:none">Left alone in Baltimore after his unpredictable lover bails, Special Agent Zane Garrett takes his frustration out on everything in his path until he is ordered to Chicago to back up an undercover operative. When he gets there, though, he finds himself face to face with his wayward partner, Special Agent Ty Grady. They have to deal with the uncertainty lingering between them while they work to retrieve their intended mark, a retired hit man and CIA wet-works operative named Julian Cross.<br /><br />Ty, once a marine and now an FBI hotshot, has a penchant for being unpredictable, a trait Zane can vouch for. Zane is a man who once lived for his job but has come to realize his heartbreaking past doesn’t have to overshadow his future. They're partners, friends, lovers, and the go-to team for unusual cases. With Cross and his innocuous boyfriend, Cameron Jacobs, in tow, Ty and Zane must navigate the obstacles of a cross-country trek, including TSA pat-downs, blizzards, their uncooperative prisoners, CIA kill teams, a desperate lack of sleep or caffeine, and each other. Ty and Zane are determined to get Julian Cross to DC in one piece, but it’s starting to look like it might be the last thing they do.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/247813398" />
    <a title="Jenn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2928214-jenn"><img alt="Jenn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1441900812p2/2928214.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/247813398?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenn" href="/user/show/2928214-jenn">Jenn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2928214-jenn?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2928214-jenn?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2928214-jenn?shelf=cops">cops</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2928214-jenn?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2928214-jenn?shelf=to-review">to-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2928214-jenn?shelf=splash-zone">splash-zone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2928214-jenn?shelf=alphas">alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2928214-jenn?shelf=beta-totally-biased">beta-totally-biased</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer247813398" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14088904726758835475">I'll probably put more of a detailed review up later. Below may have mild spoilers, read at your own risk.<br/><br/><br/>What can I say? I was one of those people that was blind rage angry at the last book. I was like explain this and that, what the fuck Nick?!?! And with this one everything was explained. The I Love You from Zane, why Nick chose to act that way, the holding back, etc.<br/><br/>The necklace is given to Ty, and it was done in a proper way. It wasn't a marriage proposal (yet), but it was a symbol from him</span>
  <span id="freeText14088904726758835475" style="display:none">I'll probably put more of a detailed review up later. Below may have mild spoilers, read at your own risk.<br /><br /><br />What can I say? I was one of those people that was blind rage angry at the last book. I was like explain this and that, what the fuck Nick?!?! And with this one everything was explained. The I Love You from Zane, why Nick chose to act that way, the holding back, etc.<br /><br />The necklace is given to Ty, and it was done in a proper way. It wasn't a marriage proposal (yet), but it was a symbol from him to Ty. It was casually done in only a way Zane could do with those amazing lovable eyes Ty could give him. <br /><br />The sex: I literally sat down and cried at the opening sex scene. It was everything to me. It had nostalgia, love, and hotness. They made comments that both of them have said throughout the series while staying in the moment. However, for a reader, having those nostalgic moments to tie back into their journey was so important. The "are you feeling this too?" Gahhhhhh, kill my heart now. It was amazing. The sex scenes/moments: is it possible you need a fan to cool off from a book? Good, lawdddyy. *pant pant*<br /><br />I hated Nick in the last book. HATED him. In this one, when I first read it I was all mehhhh. I had sympathy for his POW status, but not how he acted with Ty &amp; Zane. However, the longer I sat on it the longer everything began to fit for me. How although it may on the surface not relate: war torn anguish with real time laughter and love, it all interacts and affects how these men act and love. I got him. I felt for him. Dare I say I grew to love him? He is no threat to Ty &amp; Zane. He is a friend that loved a fellow friend for years. Now that everyone is aware of the situation he can move on. Zane can be the confident man he once was in knowing Ty is his man despite both of their faults. And deep down I would never have felt right with Ty losing his best friend over that. I"m glad too that it was done between Zane and Nick alone. <br /><br />The roadtrip: I wasn't sure I'd like that aspect, but for this book it felt right. From book 2 through 4, the boys have been stagnant. Trapped in West Virgina, on a cruise ship, and in their own emotional prison in their apartments. In this book, everything was out in the open and progressing. Their emotions, their travel, and who they were opening up with each other. It was enlightening, fun, and sigh worthy. FINALLLLLLLY.<br /><br />For those wondering about Cameron and Julian: if you were a huge fan of them before, I think this book will get you even more excited. If you weren't, well I don't think they are in it enough to be that distracting. While there is a crossover, this book is all Ty and Zane. It was nice, however, to see Ty &amp; Zane interact with individuals that were gay, not in their work field, and not family. Maybe down the road they will even have them as friends. But, Cameron and Julian are easy, and the dynamics between Julian and Ty were hilarious. Not to mention when Zane went all badass on Julian I may or may not have done a little fist pump.<br /><br />The ending. Its not a cliffhanger, but its not a HEA. How can it be with more books in the series? However, goddamnnnnnnn, its what we've been waiting for. An ending that has relationship progression that shows the readers that big decisions can come with pure joy and happiness. Yes, they know the road ahead might have some battles, but dammit they believe in each other, they are honest now, and they both know that they aren't willing to ever lose the other.<br /><br />All in all, a fantastic read!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14088904726758835475" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=memorable-favorite-heroes">memorable-favorite-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=bliss">bliss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=spellbound">spellbound</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer247815256" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15984266423168344157"><b>"Ty," Zane said between kisses, his hands firm on Ty's body. "Be mine, just for now. There's time."<br/>Ty reached for Zane's face, meeting his eyes. "I was always yours," he said with difficulty.<br/><br/>5+++++ stars.<br/><br/>Holy smokes! Kissing my Goodreads stars…kissing my Kindle…kissing Ty! Wow, wow, wow what a revelation!! Abigail had to fly solo and I'm super happy that she did such an outstanding job with Armed & Dangerous! Ladies, I'm rolling my eyes…in ecstatic delight!</b><br/><br/><i>That's love.</i><br/><br/>I loved A&D from start to f</span>
  <span id="freeText15984266423168344157" style="display:none"><b>"Ty," Zane said between kisses, his hands firm on Ty's body. "Be mine, just for now. There's time."<br />Ty reached for Zane's face, meeting his eyes. "I was always yours," he said with difficulty.<br /><br />5+++++ stars.<br /><br />Holy smokes! Kissing my Goodreads stars…kissing my Kindle…kissing Ty! Wow, wow, wow what a revelation!! Abigail had to fly solo and I'm super happy that she did such an outstanding job with Armed &amp; Dangerous! Ladies, I'm rolling my eyes…in ecstatic delight!</b><br /><br /><i>That's love.</i><br /><br />I loved A&amp;D from start to finish! Frankly, there was not one single dull moment to be found. Wonderful and well-drawn main AND secondary characters, witty dialogue and a really sensible and good plot made this story to something very special. I don't want to give away too much of the plot though. It's enough to say that Ty and Zane have to escort Julian and his lover Cameron from Chicago to Washington DC. The big question: who are the real bad guys? When they are on their <i>merry</i> way, the road gets a bit bumpy from time to time. Honestly, the prospect of a long trip on the road was not all that promising. With that said, I was pleasantly surprised that the journey was incredibly entertaining, action-packed, and utterly hilarious at times. No boredom at all. Ty and Zane <i>never</i> disappoint, that's for sure. I totally adored the way Ty and Julian were bitching at one another. My oh my, do we feel a little bit upset and cranky, my lovelies? By the way, beside Ty and Zane I really liked Julian and Cam. These two guys cranked up the fun factor tremendously! Oh, and don't forget Ty's brother Deuce. It's always a pleasure to see you again!<br /><br />Ty is the same but then again, somehow he is different. There's so much more emotional depth when these two guys are together now. Well, I don't know if it's due to their relationship development (it's the fifth book, after all) OR if it's the fact that Abigail had to fly solo when she wrote A&amp;D. Ultimately, I don't care and I'm so incredibly happy with the outcome. The love scenes are so super hot, passionate, and yet incredibly <b>intimate,</b> moving, and tender. Man, I wanted to crawl under their skin. What I especially loved as well was the kissing and touching. Lots of affectionate kissing and touching. *Le sigh*<br /><br />I adored the compass rose thingie. I just knew Zane's answer.<br /><br /><i>"Because you gave me direction when I was lost. You showed me the way." He looked up to meet Ty's eyes. "You're like my very own compass."<br />"Zane."<br />"I know, I know. I'm a sap."<br />"Maybe. But you're my sap," Ty said fondly.</i><br /><br />Further, I loved Nick and Zane's heart-to-heart. After Nick and Ty's "incident" in Divide &amp; Conquer so many readers were angry with Ty. I wasn't. I have your back, Ty. Always. That's why I was so glad that all of us got this important insight. I hope the readers will understand you way better now, Ty.<br /><br /><i>"Sometimes I…I just need a break. Up here," he said, tapping his forehead. "I have to go somewhere on my own to let life hit me. If I don't, too much piles up and…I end up not really able to deal. I just have to get away sometimes."</i><br /><br />Yeah, being a <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[tortured prisoner of war <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> can do that to you. <i>Twenty-three days, nine hours, and fifty-one minutes.</i> I'd love to know Ty's point of view. Maybe in the next book? This must have been so utterly life-changing for Ty.<br /><br />After having finished A&amp;D, I ended up smiling like a fool. It's <b>fan-freakin-tastic.</b> I'm happy.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15984266423168344157" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1394952468" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Meags" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8542123-meags"><img alt="Meags" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1524277146p2/8542123.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1394952468?book_show_action=true">Sep 18, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Meags" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Meags" href="/user/show/8542123-meags">Meags</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=panties-just-went-poof">panties-just-went-poof</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=bi-ofy-gfy">bi-ofy-gfy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=lgbt">lgbt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=assassins-and-spies">assassins-and-spies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=best-couples">best-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=crime-mystery-suspense">crime-mystery-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=law-enforcers">law-enforcers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8542123-meags?shelf=war-and-military">war-and-military</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1394952468" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17149623352366928805"><b>5 Stars</b><br/><br/>There’s just something about this series that leaves me awkwardly speechless when it comes to review writing. It’s almost been a week since I finished this story and I’m no closer to finding anything useful to say, but I’ll try.<br/><br/>I was a good little reader and read the fabulous <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6782412.Warrior_s_Cross' title='Warrior's Cross by Madeleine Urban' rel='nofollow noopener'>Warrior's Cross</a> before braving Ty and Zane’s fifth epic tale, and I’m so glad I did. I feel like so much of what made this story epic <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[what with the fantastic banter and macho stand-offs between Ty and </span></span>
  <span id="freeText17149623352366928805" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars</b><br /><br />There’s just something about this series that leaves me awkwardly speechless when it comes to review writing. It’s almost been a week since I finished this story and I’m no closer to finding anything useful to say, but I’ll try.<br /><br />I was a good little reader and read the fabulous <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6782412.Warrior_s_Cross" title="Warrior's Cross by Madeleine Urban" rel="nofollow noopener">Warrior's Cross</a> before braving Ty and Zane’s fifth epic tale, and I’m so glad I did. I feel like so much of what made this story epic <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[what with the fantastic banter and macho stand-offs between Ty and Julian <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, would have been lost somewhere in translation had I not read Julian and Cameron’s story first. It was such a treat to revisit these guys, and better yet, have them in close proximity to Ty and Zane for pretty much the entirety of this story. <br /><br />The plot for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13246997.Armed___Dangerous__Cut___Run___5_" title="Armed &amp; Dangerous (Cut &amp; Run, #5) by Abigail Roux" rel="nofollow noopener">Armed &amp; Dangerous</a> is the catalyst for such impressively action-packed, funny and romantic moments. The story sees Ty and Zane on a mission to Chicago to “detain” the illustrious Julian Cross (along with his bf Cameron), with orders to deliver him to FBI headquarters in Washington. As can only be expected in a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5199022.Cut___Run__Cut___Run___1_" title="Cut &amp; Run (Cut &amp; Run, #1) by Abigail Roux" rel="nofollow noopener">Cut &amp; Run</a> book, things don't go as planned for Ty and Zane, and soon enough their little ragtag group find themselves facing off against each other while fighting for their lives against an even bigger threat. <br /><br />Essentially, what we have here is a cross between an intense on-the-run tale of action and intrigue, and a campy road trip adventure full of good humour and romance. Needless to say, I had a blast with this particular premise.<br /><br />This fifth story also gained some serious acceleration in the romance department. I was already a Ty and Zane fanatic well before I reached this story, but man was I a goner during this particular offering. Within 15 pages I was a metaphorical puddle of goo on the floor. The love confessions were flying all over the place (YIPPEEEEE!!!) and I was in book heaven as a result; I spent a solid amount of reading time with a ridiculous grin plastered across my face, to the point that my face hurt like a bitch by the time I was done. And to be crystal clear, this book comprises some of the most epically passionate love scenes I’ve ever read - no joke!<br /><br />To say that I loved this story would be an understatement, but to say that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5199022.Cut___Run__Cut___Run___1_" title="Cut &amp; Run (Cut &amp; Run, #1) by Abigail Roux" rel="nofollow noopener">Cut &amp; Run</a> has very quickly become one of the best series I’ve ever read would be a pretty damn accurate declaration.<br /><br />******************************************<br /><br /><b>Re-read: March, 2018</b><br /><br />Loved it then, love it even more now! <br /><br />There is something about this particular installment that really solidifies the epicness of the love Ty and Zane share. It's probably because that love is now being voiced and embraced to the best of their abilities, and as a result this story is swimming in a shit-ton of tasty and swoon-worthy moments which work to elevate the romance ten-fold. <br /><br />I can confidently say that I'll never tire of reading about these guys. Nope, never!<br /><br />*dreamy sigh*<br /><br /><b>HIGHLY RECOMMENDED!!! &lt;3 </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17149623352366928805" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_397702791" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Blacky *Romance Addict*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8310179-blacky-romance-addict"><img alt="Blacky *Romance Addict*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420469509p2/8310179.jpg" /></a>

<span id="freeTextContainer188671998411641222"><b>Ty and Zane could power an entire city with how much electricity they produce together! <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=706146.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/388551.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/>Throw Julian and Cameron in the picture and you got yourself free enegry everywhere <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=311685.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/359489.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a> <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=311685.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/359489.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a> <br/><br/>This book was amazing! We get not only two absolutely fabulous characters, but 4 <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=3602195817.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/361653.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a> My mind was on overload, didn't know who to love more in every new scene <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=167153.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/361833.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a> </b><br/><br/><br/><br/>It starts right after the ending of Divide & Conquer, Ty calls Zane and appologizes, but he can't come back home bacause he's sent on a new mission. Lucky for Zane, Burns</span>
  <span id="freeText188671998411641222" style="display:none"><b>Ty and Zane could power an entire city with how much electricity they produce together! <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=706146.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/388551.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>Throw Julian and Cameron in the picture and you got yourself free enegry everywhere <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=311685.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/359489.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=311685.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/359489.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <br><br>This book was amazing! We get not only two absolutely fabulous characters, but 4 <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=3602195817.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/361653.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> My mind was on overload, didn't know who to love more in every new scene <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=167153.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/361833.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> </b><br><br><br><br>It starts right after the ending of Divide &amp; Conquer, Ty calls Zane and appologizes, but he can't come back home bacause he's sent on a new mission. Lucky for Zane, Burns sends him on the same mission to be Ty's backup <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=cheerkh2.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/374159.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> and they make up <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=bliss.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/357951.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> and at that point I was somewhere on the ground, fanited with all the swoon, it was just so lovely and beautiful and I just loved it!!! He finally gave Ty the compass <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=767622.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/362324.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=3402580550.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/362254.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> and they said "I love you" to each other again. And again. And no matter how many times they say it in the future it won't be enough <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=2783945661.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/361318.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> And in this one they pretty much made love for the first time, it wasn't just hot sex and f*cking themselves sensless :) very beautiful scene (it was hot too, don't get me wrong <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=biggestgrin_zps92d5aecd.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/372503.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> ). <br><br><br>Their mission is to force Julian Cross to come to DC and testify, but of course, Julian is a tough cookie, he doesn't want to goo back to his old job, so Ty and Zane pretty much abduct/arrest them both XD They were all hilarious together XD Julian and Ty absolutely couldn't stand each other, and they fought ALL the time, throwing jabs and insults - LOVED IT <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=355146.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/362691.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> Cameron was a sweetheart, a total nice guy caught in all the mess <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=1839924927.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/365269.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>It was a bumpy ride, trying to prevent Julian and Cameron from escaping, and then all of them trying to escape CIA/FBI operatives :) <br><br><br><br>Great story, full of dynamics, Ty and Zane's relationship progressing further <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=1839924927.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/365269.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>, Ty and Julian throwing insults <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=42kmoig.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388594ra/749194.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>, Zane dealing with Nick and Ty's past <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=468813.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/374889.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>, and Cameron being the brains in one situation which had me laughing my ass off <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=355146.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/362691.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>Just a brilliant book, confirms my addiction (obsession <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=493397.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/375337.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> ) with T&amp;Z <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=836920.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/356484.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> </b><br><br><br><br>One more thing - I strongly suggest you read <b>Warrior's Cross</b> before this one, it's the story of Julian and Cameron and it's fantastic! You won't regret it! And you'll know and love them even before you start this one <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=703126.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer12410126451243871704"><br/><br/><b>This series is like a holiday, a spa for my soul.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383227357ra/6448364.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And <b>Armed & Dangerous</b> is like the best day of it.<br/><br/><b>Ty</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383247372i/6457609._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>and <b>Zane</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383247433i/6457645.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>are not just the most <u>adorable</u> and <u>amazing</u> couple of the gay fiction, <br/>THEY ARE <b>CULT.</b> And this series is a <b>MUST READ </b> not only for the fans of M/M-genre.<br/><br/>I don’t know how Abigail Roux does it, but every sequel, every her next book is better than the previous one.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383248472ra/6458187.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> EVERYTHING IS GETTING BETTER HERE!</b><br/><br/><b>
  <u>♥ Not only the relationship</u>
</b> between Ty and Zane. <br/>There are no misunderstandings. <br/>They spea</span>
  <span id="freeText12410126451243871704" style="display:none"><br><br><b>This series is like a holiday, a spa for my soul.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383227357ra/6448364.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And <b>Armed &amp; Dangerous</b> is like the best day of it.<br><br><b>Ty</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383247372i/6457609._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and <b>Zane</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383247433i/6457645.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>are not just the most <u>adorable</u> and <u>amazing</u> couple of the gay fiction, <br>THEY ARE <b>CULT.</b> And this series is a <b>MUST READ </b> not only for the fans of M/M-genre.<br><br>I don’t know how Abigail Roux does it, but every sequel, every her next book is better than the previous one.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383248472ra/6458187.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> EVERYTHING IS GETTING BETTER HERE!</b><br><br><b>
  <u>♥ Not only the relationship</u>

  <u>♥ Not only sex.</u>
</b> <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383249186ra/6458475.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh yeah...Sex deserves only superlatives! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/482596.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The sex scenes are one of the best I have ever read.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382669938ra/6110463.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>♥ Though also a <b>suspense part!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383248799ra/6458365.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, you can forget the weakest point of the first books!!<br>There is nothing of a B-action movie in it! <br>The plot turned into an excellent thriller. <br><b>Nothing predictable, nothing secondary, nothing insignificant.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384078870ra/6765082.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>♥ It is a perfect mixture out of a <b>heartbreaking romance</b>, an <b>action thriller</b>, a <b>mind-blowing erotic</b> and a warm sweet romantic <b>comedy</b>!<br> <br><b>FANTASTIC READING EXPERIENCE!</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383257754ra/6463119.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I ENJOYED EVERY SINGLE MOMENT OF THIS BOOK!<br>IT IS FUN!<br>IT IS A GOOD MOOD!<br>IT IS SMILE ON MY FACE ALL DAY LONG!!</b> <br><br><b>
  <u>I CAN'T HAVE ENOUGH OF TY AND ZANE! <br>AND I WANT MORE!!!!!!!!!!!</u>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3478870662" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3970875883488409477">This one was like Vacation or Planes, Trains, and Automobiles (80's movies. Look it up, kids). A comedy of errors with guns, killing, an over-zealous TSA agent in rubber gloves, and more handcuffs and ropes than a BDSM convention. In other words, lots of fun.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1596957040i/29938403._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Yes, just like this but with less childhood trauma.<br/><br/>Ty and Zane are tasked with bringing in two guys that we met in the spin-off book, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6782412.Warrior_s_Cross' title='Warrior's Cross by Madeleine Urban' rel='nofollow noopener'>Warrior's Cross</a>. One of them is a deadly, gorgeous, highly skilled assassin. The other is his boyfriend - a</span>
  <span id="freeText3970875883488409477" style="display:none">This one was like Vacation or Planes, Trains, and Automobiles (80's movies. Look it up, kids). A comedy of errors with guns, killing, an over-zealous TSA agent in rubber gloves, and more handcuffs and ropes than a BDSM convention. In other words, lots of fun.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1596957040i/29938403._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes, just like this but with less childhood trauma.<br><br>Ty and Zane are tasked with bringing in two guys that we met in the spin-off book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6782412.Warrior_s_Cross" title="Warrior's Cross by Madeleine Urban" rel="nofollow noopener">Warrior's Cross</a>. One of them is a deadly, gorgeous, highly skilled assassin. The other is his boyfriend - a waiter who is constantly described as small and "average looking." Okay, whatever floats your boat. These two guys are not going to come willingly with Ty and Zane, so hijinx abound since the assassin is so darn skilled and deadly and whatnot.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1596957119ra/29938424.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>No cage can hold him, baby.<br><br>There was a lot of action and hilarious moments, and since I had read the other book I enjoyed both couples. It was hard to know whether to root for them to escape, or not escape. I wanted them all to win, and maybe everyone get a trophy and stuff.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1596957040ra/29938402.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Pizza party for everyone!<br><br>The only thing I didn't like was the very last line in the book. That sucked.</span>

<div id="review_2661601113" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2661601113" />
    <a title="Nancy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/763271-nancy"><img alt="Nancy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435597527p2/763271.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2661601113?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nancy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nancy" href="/user/show/763271-nancy">Nancy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/763271-nancy?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/763271-nancy?shelf=lgbt">lgbt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/763271-nancy?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/763271-nancy?shelf=shelf-inflicted">shelf-inflicted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/763271-nancy?shelf=january-challenge">january-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2661601113" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1694172002534804950"><b>Posted at <a href='http://www.shelfinflicted.com/2019/04/armed-and-dangerous.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Shelf Inflicted</a></b><br/><br/>I think I’m done with Ty and Zane.<br/><br/>In this fifth book of the Cut & Run series, it seems that one half of the author duo is now going it alone. And the other half has absconded with the Ty and Zane I loved in the earlier books. <br/><br/>Don’t get me wrong. I’m happy that Ty and Zane are now at the stage of their relationship where they have found a happy equilibrium. The problem is, their behavior is so out of character, especially after Ty’s sudden departure in the last book. Forg</span>
  <span id="freeText1694172002534804950" style="display:none"><b>Posted at <a href="http://www.shelfinflicted.com/2019/04/armed-and-dangerous.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Shelf Inflicted</a></b><br /><br />I think I’m done with Ty and Zane.<br /><br />In this fifth book of the Cut &amp; Run series, it seems that one half of the author duo is now going it alone. And the other half has absconded with the Ty and Zane I loved in the earlier books. <br /><br />Don’t get me wrong. I’m happy that Ty and Zane are now at the stage of their relationship where they have found a happy equilibrium. The problem is, their behavior is so out of character, especially after Ty’s sudden departure in the last book. Forgiveness happened a little too quickly for my liking, and the excessive declarations of love, the “oh, baby’s” and humming by most of the male characters made me want to stick a fork in my eye. <br /><br /><u>Number of hums</u><br />Ty Grady – 10<br />Zane Garrett – 6<br />Julian Cross – 5<br />Cameron Jacobs – 2<br />Nick O’Flaherty – 1<br />Richard Burns – 1<br /><br />These guys are supposed to be badass. Instead, they are sitting around talking about feelings! I miss the verbal sparring and the snarky humor of the earlier books. The action scenes, though, are as ridiculous and unrealistic as always. While I was able to overlook that before, I am unable to do so now. <br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>“Julian struck out at him so quickly it was easy to think it was imagined. He grabbed the gun and pulled the slide, his free hand moving in a flash, and the gun fell apart in Leatherface’s hand. Julian swung at him with the slide, hitting him in the temple and dropping him in a heap.”</blockquote>
</i><br /><br />This scene confuses me. No matter how scrappy Julian may be, I seriously doubt he would be able to disarm a rogue CIA agent, strip the slide off his pistol and knock him unconscious. If Julian grabbed the gun to pull the slide, wouldn’t the gun be in Julian’s hand? And while many guns may be designed to be quick and easy to disassemble, they don’t just “fall apart” in someone’s hand. <br /><br />Unlike earlier books where the focus was on the main couple, we are introduced to two new characters, Julian Cross (the only witness to a contract killing) who Ty and Zane must bring to DC in one piece, and his milquetoast boyfriend, Cameron Jacobs. <br /><br />The lengthy road trip undertaken by these four guys while Julian and Cameron were often restrained was excruciatingly slow. I quickly tired of their banter. I skimmed through the sex scenes, which were drawn out and repetitive. Julian’s cats, Smith and Wesson, were a nice touch. I hope Ty and Zane get permanent custody. <br /><br />Since I have the next book on my Kindle, I’ll probably read it. But I don’t have high expectations.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1694172002534804950" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer247841072" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6745812083425497124">Some readers said they had resigned themselves to not expecting too much from this book, since it's not, as the previous ones, the product of the collaboration between Madeleine Urban & Abigail Roux. I can proudly say I was not among them. I DID expect a lot, because I knew Abigail Roux's an amazing author. One of the very best, whether she works with or without a co-author. But Jesus Christ Almighty, not even in my wildest dreams did I expect this book to actually be so freaking awesome and <i>exc</i></span>
  <span id="freeText6745812083425497124" style="display:none">Some readers said they had resigned themselves to not expecting too much from this book, since it's not, as the previous ones, the product of the collaboration between Madeleine Urban &amp; Abigail Roux. I can proudly say I was not among them. I DID expect a lot, because I knew Abigail Roux's an amazing author. One of the very best, whether she works with or without a co-author. But Jesus Christ Almighty, not even in my wildest dreams did I expect this book to actually be so freaking awesome and <i>exceed</i> all my expectations!! So if you have any lingering doubts as to whether this book is worth reading, just do yourself a favour and give up on them. Go and buy this book, and prepare for THE RIDE OF YOUR LIFE!!!!! If Ty &amp; Zane together with Julian &amp; Cameron won't rock your world than nothing, abso-bloody-lutely nothing can!<br /><br />Now on to the actual review, which, by the way, <b>contains <u>SPOILERS</u>, so if you haven't read the book yet, but still want to read this review, you're doing it at your own risk.</b><br /><br />Those who know me certainly remember my reaction to <i>Divide &amp; Conquer</i>. While I loved that book, some events, especially the Nick <i>incident</i> left me seething. It didn't help that Ty ignored the first time Zane said he loved him. I tried to rationalize, justify Ty's behaviour, his reaction to that one and so many other things, including, of course, the ending and why he left. Finally, I came to terms with <i>almost</i> everything that happend in that book. Yep, almost. The name Nick. Ringing a bell? <br /><br />Okay, so that was how I saw things after reading <i>Divide &amp; Conquer</i> (full review of book 4 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/199367259" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>).<br /><br /><i>Armed &amp; Dangerous</i> opens a new chapter in Ty &amp; Zane's relationship. It's truly amazing how far these guys have come and how much their relationship has progressed. Zane is much more confident, no longer living in the past, no longer denying his feelings. And yet, there's still a lingering vulnerability somewhere deep inside him. He knows that Ty loves him. There can never be any doubt about it. Still... when he finds out the whole truth about the kiss, when Ty tells Zane that he kissed Nick back and enjoyed it, Zane feels like he's been punched. Hard. And every time the name Nick O'Flaherty comes up something inside Zane's chest twists. I really felt for Zane. He finally left the past behind only to have his present and future overshadowed by fear that Nick O'Flaherty may try to steal Ty away from him. And then, of course, comes O'Flaherty himself. And THE TALK between him and Zane, without Ty being present. And OMG! The things that have been revealed! Jesus Christ! I was stunned speechless!!!! I HATED Nick after <i>D&amp;C</i> but now I just can't. What happened in Afghanistan and Nick's silence soon after, the reason he didn't tell Ty about his feelings is now crystal clear. Obviously, I'm glad he didn't tell Ty then he loved him, but nobody deserves to go through the shit Ty and Nick went through together. Nobody. Besides, now that I know Nick is no longer a threat to Ty &amp; Zane's relationship I find myself sympathizing with him (dare I say it?: liking him, or even if I'm not there yet, I will get to that point soon, I think).<br /><br />"<i>Nick nodded and swallowed hard. “I was in love with him. I’d already made up my mind to tell him after our tour was over. Consequences be damned, I just needed him to know. But after that….” He shook his head and cleared his throat. “There are some friends you don’t risk for your own peace of mind. Some things… at the time it wasn’t worth the risk of losing him.” <br /><br />“Last month when you….” <br /><br />“I knew I’d already lost him.” </i>"<br /><br /><br /><br />"<i>(...) if you’re asking if I intend to make another move on him, the answer’s no. I’ve regretted what I did every day since.” </i>"<br /><br />Oh, and I absolutely loved that Nick actually helped Zane to understand Ty better. He didn't have to give Zane the CDs with some films from when Ty and Nick and their other Recon buddies had been in service. But he did. If this isn't an olive branch, a peace offering, if this doesn't scream 'I'm sorry, I won't try anything like this ever again. You make Ty happy and I want us to get along', than I don't know what does. And I guess it's good that they are trying. Ty confessed to missing his best friend, though if he had to choose he would <i>always</i> choose Zane, but why make him do it?<br /><br />So, the Nick issue is no longer a problem. Whoa, I <i>really</i> had it bad after <i>D&amp;C</i> if I'm making this all about Nick, but bear with me, will you? I really <i>had to</i> get it out of my system.<br /><br />Okay, back to the relationship stuff. I loved that Ty &amp; Zane decided to share with each other things about their pasts. No more secrets. No more hiding. They are more open with each other. Every single time one of them said 'I Love You' I had this silly grin on my face, which means I was grinning A LOT! :D <br /><br />And the sex, no, scratch that, because it was not just sex or f*cking, but MAKING LOVE! Such tenderness! And the connection they share! *sighs* God, so beautiful! I DIED AND WENT TO HEAVEN!!! And FINALLY what we all were waiting for: Ty bottoming! SQUEEEEEEEEE!!! So perfect! I had happy tears in my eyes while reading that scene. ALL the sex scenes were hot and earth-shattering! So much passion and love:<br /><br />"<i>“Ty,” Zane said as he released Ty’s other wrist and moved his hand to splay his palm across Ty’s chest. “Look at me. Open your eyes, baby.” </i><br /><br />"<i>Zane swallowed hard as he drew a shaky breath. “Are you feeling this too?” he asked (...). <br /><br />“Yes,” Ty answered, surprised at how desperate the honest answer sounded.(...) He couldn’t hear a thing but his own heartbeat. “I’ll always be yours, baby.” </i>"<br /><br />*sighs* Yep, it's official, I'm a sap. But who cares?! It's TY &amp; ZANE!!!!<br /><br />And Lord, was I happy that Zane gave Ty the necklace! FINALLLLLYYYYYYYY!!! :D And when Zane explained to Ty its meaning, how Ty was like his compass, and then the sap comment delivered with fondness, awwwww, so romantic! *sighs*<br /><br />Uhm, I think I've calmed myself enough to continue. <br /><br />Damn, this review is way too long and I have yet to mention Julian and Cameron. Let me tell you this: I loved Julian in <i>Warrior's Cross</i>, but here I REALLY, REALLY LOVED the guy! The wit! The sarcasm! Now enter a very pissed, in kill mode and on Red Bull, Special Agent, Ty Grady and... BANG!!! I LOVED, LOVED their banter! God, some comments that came out of Julian's mouth! *snickers* Priceless! And Cam with his constant never-knows-when-to-shut-up chattering and the "<i>“Ty is like… a ninja on crack. </i>" comment made me laugh so hard that I thanked God nobody was home and saw me. They would think me batshit crazy, LOL<br /><br />Oh, and I loved Smith and Wesson! :D<br /><br />All right, I'm wrapping this up. There's only one thing left to say and that would be the ending. No cliff-hanger this time! :D Our boys get a solid Happy For Now ending, which shows that although a lot has already changed for the better, there are some things that still need working on, like coming out to their FBI co-workers, which seems not a best thing to do. Not yet. But hey! Zane is moving in with Ty! *happy dance* (if their co-workers ask, Zane rents a room *shrug*). But progress is progress and each new book brings us closer to a true Happily Ever After that Ty &amp; Zane so deserve - and which I have no doubt Abigail Roux will finally grant them.<br /><br />All in all, <i>Armed &amp; Dangerous</i> is a fabulous read. A spectacular book, which is definitely my favourite in the whole series. <b>5 + stars</b>.<br /><br /><br />Abigail, thank you. I can't even put into words how much the fact that you keep writing this series despite Madeleine's decision to stop her writing career means to us, readers. You truly are an amazing writer and a wonderful person. Thank you! *hugs*</span>
  <a data-text-id="6745812083425497124" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Optimist ♰King&#39;s Wench♰" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Optimist ♰King&#39;s Wench♰" href="/user/show/12766897-optimist-king-s-wench">Optimist ♰King&#39;s Wench♰</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Optimist ♰King's Wench♰ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/1969357-jane-ps">Jane (PS)</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12766897-optimist-king-s-wench?shelf=boys-who-like-boys">boys-who-like-boys</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer469678238" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4588094261148958543"><b>11/7/18 re-listen</b><br/><br/>I still really enjoyed this one for it's relationship development and romantic suspense. I actually really enjoyed Cam's role in this one unlike my first rodeo. *shrugs*<br/><br/>I also think I'd put this at 4 stars rather than 5. I seem to be getting finicky or maybe it's fickle? Tomato, to-mah-toe.<br/><br/>Crisden did an excellent job with the narration. He gave everyone a distinct voice so I never got confused as to who was talking and even did some accents!<br/><br/>************Original Review**********</span>
  <span id="freeText4588094261148958543" style="display:none"><b>11/7/18 re-listen</b><br /><br />I still really enjoyed this one for it's relationship development and romantic suspense. I actually really enjoyed Cam's role in this one unlike my first rodeo. *shrugs*<br /><br />I also think I'd put this at 4 stars rather than 5. I seem to be getting finicky or maybe it's fickle? Tomato, to-mah-toe.<br /><br />Crisden did an excellent job with the narration. He gave everyone a distinct voice so I never got confused as to who was talking and even did some accents!<br /><br />************Original Review************<br /><br />When I started <i>Armed &amp; Dangerous</i> it was with a good deal of trepidation and an even great degree of peevishness. You see, Ty has been my knight in shining armor since <i>Cut &amp; Run</i>. My Superman. He could do no wrong until <i>Divide &amp; Conquer</i>. So, not only did he need to redeem himself with Zane, he needed to redeem himself with me and he did. In spades.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>“I love you,” Ty said, the quiet words devoid of any self-consciousness or his usual bravado. “And I’ve never been able to say that before with such conviction. I can’t remember a time that you weren’t the first thing I thought of, and I want to spend the rest of my life with you. I don’t care what stands in our way.”</blockquote>
</b><br /><br /><i>Better. More groveling, please.</i><br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>“I’ll always be yours, baby.”</blockquote>
</b><br /><br /><i>Oh alright, you're forgiven. But, don't let it happen again.</i><br /><br />Ms. Roux has some kind of special magic to continue to achieve this level of entertainment in a continuing series. In my humble opinion, it just continues to get better between these two knuckleheads. How she and her usual co-author, Ms. Urban, have managed to avoid the doldrums, I've no idea but kudos to them.<br /><br />I'd characterize this installment as the most romantic thus far with both Ty and Zane declaring themselves, sharing their feelings and even discussing expectations for the future. All things they've managed to avoid, for the most part, until now. Don't misunderstand me, this is Ty and Zane's version of romance which usually includes a fist fight, one or both getting shot, sometimes ending up in the hospital, coloring outside the lines in a legal sense and they are probably going to rack up a body count. *shrug* That's how they roll.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>Ty sighed, an almost inaudible release of air. The look in Zane’s eyes was something Ty had never seen. It was intense and heated, possessive, filled with emotion that made Ty’s chest hurt all over again, like the first time he’d ever looked into that fire in Zane’s eyes and known that there would be no one else in the world for him.</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />Though it was nice to have some background information on Julian and Cam, I continue to stand by my review of <i>Warrior's Cross</i>. Actually, I'm not completely convinced the pertinent information wasn't provided here. The most entertaining part was adding Julian to the mix and getting to be a fly on the wall for Ty and Julian's interactions. Ty is <b>always</b> hilarious but him and Julian together? Good Lord! I laughed out loud many, many times. My pick for best conversation between them:<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>“Fine,” Julian said, his tone making it clear he was reaching the end of his patience. “We’ll solve this like men.”<br /><br />“What do you want, MacGuffin, a duel?”<br /><br />“No.” Julian held out both hands, one palm flat, the other held over it in a fist. “Rock, paper, scissors. Two out of three.”<br /><br />Ty rolled his eyes and held out his fist, apparently willing to play. Julian hit his palm three times, and Ty kept time with his fist in the air. But when Julian threw a paper, Ty reached into his jacket with his other hand and pulled his gun, aiming it at Julian.<br /><br />“Ty!” Zane said in exasperation from the front seat.<br /><br />“Glock, paper, scissors. I win."</blockquote>
</b><br /><br /><i>No, Ty, we all win!</i><br /><br />Cam managed to prove himself to be just this side of window dressing. I will give him credit for keeping his cool through all the shenanigans and his ingenuity in a crunch.<br /><br />The action aspect of <i>Armed &amp; Dangerous</i> was entertaining enough although, I still think <i>Cut &amp; Run</i> was the best plot line of the series. Nick and Deuce make appearances and Nick provides some painful insights into Ty. We actually learned quite a bit about Ty, some about Zane, both of which set things up nicely for the future. Still, the character and relationship development are what keep me coming back for more. Well, that and the sexy times. I tell you what, the sexy times are few and far between in these books but… Wow! Patience is rewarded with long, slow, thorough, visceral and achingly erotic scenes.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>"Ty whimpered at the tone of Zane’s voice and the promise in it. “I should do this for you more often,” he said in a tortured voice.<br /><br />“Do what?”<br /><br />“Give you everything I have.”</blockquote>
</b><br /><br /><br />All of these elements combined to make <i>Armed &amp; Dangerous</i> yet another 5 star book in the <i>Cut &amp; Run</i> series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4588094261148958543" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/793510189?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shurrn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shurrn" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn">Shurrn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=genre-crime-or-mystery">genre-crime-or-mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=i-lgbt">i-lgbt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=romance-suspense">romance-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=c-playing-detective">c-playing-detective</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=romance-mm">romance-mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=c-favorite-males">c-favorite-males</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=i-lol-moments">i-lol-moments</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=romance-modern">romance-modern</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=z-own-for-kindle">z-own-for-kindle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer793510189" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12594859718216521382"><b>Wonderful twists and turns; a wild ride befitting this cross-country mission, and cameo appearances all over the place!</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392435ra/755438.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Ty had been told not long ago that he shouldn't enjoy the almost-getting-killed part of his job as much as he did. Zane didn't know who had said it, but ever since, Ty had been making a concerted effort to hide his unholy glee during melees.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> This installment of the Cut & Run series is a journey which pits the FBI against the CIA...<br/><i><br/>Corrupt government officials,<br/>A cont</i></span>
  <span id="freeText12594859718216521382" style="display:none"><b>Wonderful twists and turns; a wild ride befitting this cross-country mission, and cameo appearances all over the place!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392435ra/755438.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Ty had been told not long ago that he shouldn't enjoy the almost-getting-killed part of his job as much as he did. Zane didn't know who had said it, but ever since, Ty had been making a concerted effort to hide his unholy glee during melees.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> This installment of the Cut &amp; Run series is a journey which pits the FBI against the CIA...<br><i><br>Corrupt government officials,<br>A contract killer,<br>A clueless boyfriend,<br>Bomb threats,<br>Stolen vehicles,<br>Cavity searches,<br>Five States,<br>Four dogs,<br>two giant cats,<br>&amp; some of the hottest Ty &amp; Zane moments ever...</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381413874ra/4832055.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>(Note: I recommend reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6782412.Warrior_s_Cross" title="Warrior's Cross by Madeleine Urban" rel="nofollow noopener">Warrior's Cross</a> before this book so you have the benefit of Cam &amp; Julian's backstory. It's not required, but it will enhance your enjoyment.)</i><br><br>Our boys have been called on a Black Ops mission by Director Burns. The Mission: Escort Julian Cross from Chicago to DC without anyone getting killed... As usual with Ty &amp; Zane the non-killing/dying clause in their mission is not an easy one to accomplish...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397065622ra/9225835.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We get several cameos from beloved characters seen in previous books:<br> - Cameron and Julian from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6782412.Warrior_s_Cross" title="Warrior's Cross by Madeleine Urban" rel="nofollow noopener">Warrior's Cross</a>.<br> - Nick O'Flaherty from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12384681.Divide___Conquer__Cut___Run___4_" title="Divide &amp; Conquer (Cut &amp; Run, #4) by Abigail Roux" rel="nofollow noopener">Divide &amp; Conquer</a><br> - Deuce Grady from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7314827.Sticks___Stones__Cut___Run___2_" title="Sticks &amp; Stones (Cut &amp; Run, #2) by Abigail Roux" rel="nofollow noopener">Sticks &amp; Stones</a><br>The cameos served to make all those gentlemen even more lovable... I even have an admiration for Nick despite his unflattering behavior in the last book...<br><br>In the midst of all the danger, Ty &amp; Zane are moving forward in their relationship. They're sharing secrets and becoming more tender, and the love between the two is a wonderful thing to see... Though they still have moments where they want to strangle each other.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380414800ra/818140.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The plot line in this one kept me guessing until the very end - much like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5199022.Cut___Run__Cut___Run___1_" title="Cut &amp; Run (Cut &amp; Run, #1) by Abigail Roux" rel="nofollow noopener">Cut &amp; Run</a>... I do love a book with enough mystery to add to the thrill of the mission. <br><br><i>The romance was spectacular.<br>The humor was perfection.<br>The characters were outstanding.<br>The suspense was amazing...</i><br><br>I have officially added this series to my <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=favorite-romantic-series" rel="nofollow noopener">Favorite Romantic Series Shelf</a>! It took me five books and one spin-off to solidify my devotion to the series... Much like Ty &amp; Zane's relationship, it has been a gradual buildup into an unstoppable love for me.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385506i/744465._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'd like to thank Wendy (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts" rel="nofollow noopener">Wendy's Thoughts</a>) for sending me a beautiful gift: The final books in this series. Sending someone a book is like sending them a hug. I'm overjoyed and immensely thankful.<br><br><b>
  <u>My Other Reviews in the Cut &amp; Run Series:</u>

<div id="review_2656167503" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2656167503" />
    <a title="Gerbera_Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/68687480-gerbera-reads"><img alt="Gerbera_Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578061403p2/68687480.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2656167503?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gerbera_Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gerbera_Reads" href="/user/show/68687480-gerbera-reads">Gerbera_Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=crime">crime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=awesome">awesome</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=nemesis">nemesis</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=great-read">great-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=one-of-the-best">one-of-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=must-read">must-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2656167503" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1642253453876783308">Reread January 2020.<br/><br/>I loved rereading this book especially that hotel scene in Gettysburg. It was so sweet and sexy! I enjoyed the humor, the characters, the fast pace. Contrary to some complainers, I like how Ty and Zane's relationship changed and became settled and gentle. I don't know why people expected them to be at each other's throats after professing their feelings, plus both men changed since they first met! For me those sweet nicknames, their quiet moments when they shared past and sec</span>
  <span id="freeText1642253453876783308" style="display:none">Reread January 2020.<br /><br />I loved rereading this book especially that hotel scene in Gettysburg. It was so sweet and sexy! I enjoyed the humor, the characters, the fast pace. Contrary to some complainers, I like how Ty and Zane's relationship changed and became settled and gentle. I don't know why people expected them to be at each other's throats after professing their feelings, plus both men changed since they first met! For me those sweet nicknames, their quiet moments when they shared past and secrets were the best! I do not care much about Julian and Cameron as a couple but Ty and Julian as verbal sparring partners - yes please! And I really liked Ty and Deuce getting a little more page time in the book. I always liked Deuce - he is such opposite to Ty, but the way the author shows their affection for each other through humor and little conversations they manage to sneak in between the events is perfect! Awww, love my men Ty and Zane! <br /><br />***<br /><br />I love reading series about one couple and see how their relationship evolves with time, and it can't get any better than this. Ty and Zane are so in love and finally are able to express it. Their intimate moments were so profound and passionate, so beautiful and I seriously didn't want the book to end. I am slayed and I converted myself to Ty and Zane's devotee. <br /><br />This time the simple case of grab and deliver turns into run for you life and don't get dead again. The trouble magnet duo is joined by a pair consisting of loving deadly assassin Julian Cross and his partner Cameron who believes that Julian is the best thing since sugar. Somewhere during their adventures enemies turn into friends, and grudging respect turns into admiration. The humor and sarcasm were flying like ping pong ball between Ty and Julian with Zane and Cameron being constant spectators, and I loved every page of it. Some of the time I thought they would not make it simply because one of them would snap but in the end all it took was loyalty and Wesson to sway Julian's opinion. <br /><br />Anyway, I loved this book, I loved the characters - all of them. There were secrets shared that were painful but necessary to know, trust established and new bonds forged. It was all great, and now I am off to the next one! Highly recommend it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1642253453876783308" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1053824376" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8429133091951802241">I am going to keep this short since there are so many reviews out there for this little gem. I absolutely loved it. Up until this book, I had a hard time feeling Ty and Zane’s true feeling towards one another. This book has all the feels!! They were sweet, funny, and I could finally see the connection they had. <br/><br/>Ty and Zane are off to Chicago to bring in a CIA “contact” back to D.C. Of course, it is just another adventure for Ty and Zane. This contact is dangerous, and it takes all Ty and Zane’s </span>
  <span id="freeText8429133091951802241" style="display:none">I am going to keep this short since there are so many reviews out there for this little gem. I absolutely loved it. Up until this book, I had a hard time feeling Ty and Zane’s true feeling towards one another. This book has all the feels!! They were sweet, funny, and I could finally see the connection they had. <br /><br />Ty and Zane are off to Chicago to bring in a CIA “contact” back to D.C. Of course, it is just another adventure for Ty and Zane. This contact is dangerous, and it takes all Ty and Zane’s resources to keep everyone alive. <br /><br />I <b>highly</b> recommend you read <i>Warrior’s Cross</i> before you start <i>Armed &amp; Dangerous</i>. It will definitely help you understand and enjoy A &amp; R even more.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8429133091951802241" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <a title="Cristina T." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cristina T." href="/user/show/21090104-cristina-t">Cristina T.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/14740364-armed-dangerous">review of another edition</a>
