        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer761597693" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer744846429006316851">Absolutely epic! This book is my favorite in the series so far.<br/><br/>Recipe for perfection? Take Ty & Zane, add Julian & Cam (<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8687842.Warrior_s_Cross' title='Warrior's Cross by Madeleine Urban' rel='nofollow noopener'>Warrior's Cross</a>) to the mix, sprinkle with Nick O'Flaherty (<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12877181.Divide___Conquer__Cut___Run___4_' title='Divide & Conquer (Cut & Run, #4) by Madeleine Urban' rel='nofollow noopener'>Divide & Conquer</a>) and Deuce Grady (<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8706986.Sticks___Stones__Cut___Run___2_' title='Sticks & Stones (Cut & Run, #2) by Madeleine Urban' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sticks & Stones</a>). For more flavor, throw in a road trip and shake it all up. Et voilà! Bon appetit!<br/><br/>I don't want to spoil the plot, so I'm gonna keep this short. Ty & Zane get a new assignment from Burns, specifically to escort Julian Cross to Washington DC. Julian refuses to go withou</span>
  <span id="freeText744846429006316851" style="display:none">Absolutely epic! This book is my favorite in the series so far.<br /><br />Recipe for perfection? Take Ty &amp; Zane, add Julian &amp; Cam (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8687842.Warrior_s_Cross" title="Warrior's Cross by Madeleine Urban" rel="nofollow noopener">Warrior's Cross</a>) to the mix, sprinkle with Nick O'Flaherty (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12877181.Divide___Conquer__Cut___Run___4_" title="Divide &amp; Conquer (Cut &amp; Run, #4) by Madeleine Urban" rel="nofollow noopener">Divide &amp; Conquer</a>) and Deuce Grady (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8706986.Sticks___Stones__Cut___Run___2_" title="Sticks &amp; Stones (Cut &amp; Run, #2) by Madeleine Urban" rel="nofollow noopener">Sticks &amp; Stones</a>). For more flavor, throw in a road trip and shake it all up. Et voilà! Bon appetit!<br /><br />I don't want to spoil the plot, so I'm gonna keep this short. Ty &amp; Zane get a new assignment from Burns, specifically to escort Julian Cross to Washington DC. Julian refuses to go without his lover, Cameron, because he wants to keep him safe. Of course, with Ty &amp; Zane's history, the trip is anything but safe. At first, Julian keeps trying to escape, but then he realizes that Ty &amp; Zane are the good guys and they earn his respect. So, they fight as a team against the enemy.<br /><br />I'm so glad I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8687842.Warrior_s_Cross" title="Warrior's Cross by Madeleine Urban" rel="nofollow noopener">Warrior's Cross</a> before this one, since it helped me understand Julian &amp; Cam better. They worked so well together, drawing strength from each other, supporting and loving one another, just like Ty &amp; Zane. Having all four MCs together was a lot of fun! I loved their conversations; Ty &amp; Julian bitching at each other; Zane &amp; Cam being hilarious - it was a fun ride!<br /><br />After the cliffy ending of the last book, we get some insight into Ty's mind and Zane gets the answers he needs. Their time apart has changed Ty in a good way and it has only managed to make their relationship stronger. The sex scenes were hotter than ever, but at the same time Ty &amp; Zane were also more tender and much more intimate, expressing their love without boundaries. They also enjoyed their stolen moments where they could do simple gestures like holding hands, without the fear of being recognized in a strange city.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>"Baby," Ty whispered against Zane's lips. He had never felt this sort of heat and longing for another person. He didn't know how Zane did it, but Ty knew that there would never be anyone else for him. He wanted Zane to feel that too, to have that assurance both physically and emotionally. He would do whatever he had to do to make sure that Zane knew he was his.</b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>"I love you. I will always be yours, Zane–no matter where I am or where you are. I promise you that," he said, the words as serious as Zane had ever heard Ty utter.</b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Ty looks at his partner as if he can see right into his soul sometimes. Zane has asked himself repeatedly what his lover sees in him and we finally get an answer...<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>Anyone with any sense would have steered clear. But from the first moment Ty had really looked into Zane's eyes, he's seen behind them, into the man Zane was capable of being. He's seen a phoenix waiting to rise from the ashes, and he still did. Every time he looked into Zane, he saw something extraordinary.</b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Another thing which played with my emotions was Zane &amp; Nick's conversation about Ty &amp; Nick's past <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[as tortured war prisoners, which lasted for twenty-three days, nine hours, and fifty-one minutes. That's a long ride through hell and my heart broke for Nick &amp; Ty. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I didn't blame Nick for his actions before, but I appreciated his apology to Zane anyway. I just couldn't and still can't hate this guy; Nick's just awesome!<br /><br />Oh, I almost forgot! Zane FINALLY gave Ty the rose compass he bought a while ago and I was grinning like an idiot throughout the whole scene...<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>"Why a compass?" Ty asked. [...]<br />"Because you gave me direction when I was lost. You showed me the way." He looked up to meet Ty's eyes. "You're like my very own compass."<br />"Zane."<br />"I know, I know. I'm a sap."<br />"Maybe. But you're my sap," Ty said fondly.</b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Fantastic reading experience! I just can't get enough of Ty &amp; Zane!<br /><br />* * * * *<br /><br /><i>First read: May, 2014<br />Re-read: May, 2015</i><br /><br />* * * * *<br /><br /><br /><b>My other reviews in the Cut &amp; Run series:</b><br /><i>will be updated as soon as new books are published</i><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5199023.Cut___Run__Cut___Run___1_" title="Cut &amp; Run (Cut &amp; Run, #1) by Madeleine Urban" rel="nofollow noopener">Cut &amp; <div id="review_323728289" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/323728289" />
    <a title="Lisa Arbitrary - AttentionIsArbitrary M/M Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7192208-lisa-arbitrary---attentionisarbitrary-m-m-blog"><img alt="Lisa Arbitrary - AttentionIsArbitrary M/M Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544994929p2/7192208.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/323728289?book_show_action=true">May 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa Arbitrary - AttentionIsArbitrary M/M Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa Arbitrary - AttentionIsArbitrary M/M Blog" href="/user/show/7192208-lisa-arbitrary---attentionisarbitrary-m-m-blog">Lisa Arbitrary - AttentionIsArbitrary M/M Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">m-m, fbi, spy, assassin, romancel</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7192208-lisa-arbitrary---attentionisarbitrary-m-m-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7192208-lisa-arbitrary---attentionisarbitrary-m-m-blog?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7192208-lisa-arbitrary---attentionisarbitrary-m-m-blog?shelf=m-m-romance">m-m-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer323728289" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16162536529065595729">~~~<br/><br/><b>
  <u>A Gift!</u>
</b> <br/><br/>This book is a gift given by the author to the reader. It is full of exquisite romance, passion-filled exchanges and quirky little quips and phrases that are exactly what we love about Ty and Zane.<br/><br/>"Less talky, Zane,"<br/>"I don't think I've ever been gayer than I am right now."<br/>"Come on, Zane, don't be scared of a little pussy,"<br/>_____________________<br/><br/>"This was like National Lampoon's Vacation, but with death, property destruction, and an Irish accent." <br/><br/><b>The Adventure:</b> is twisted and involv</span>
  <span id="freeText16162536529065595729" style="display:none">~~~<br><br><b>
  <u>A Gift!</u>
</b> <br><br>This book is a gift given by the author to the reader. It is full of exquisite romance, passion-filled exchanges and quirky little quips and phrases that are exactly what we love about Ty and Zane.<br><br>"Less talky, Zane,"<br>"I don't think I've ever been gayer than I am right now."<br>"Come on, Zane, don't be scared of a little pussy,"<br>_____________________<br><br>"This was like National Lampoon's Vacation, but with death, property destruction, and an Irish accent." <br><br><b>The Adventure:</b> is twisted and involved enough to keep the reader on their toes and not really seeing what is to come. Plus, what's not to love about putting four gay men in a car, on a road-trip of sorts who on some level all despise or at least don't trust each other. It's great fun to see what will happen.<br><br>______________________<br><br>Even the personality of the cats ring through - "Smith and Wesson both sat down in the opening to bedroom, ready to enjoy the show".<br><br><b>The Characters:</b> are all just perfect, well developed and likeable/loveable. We read this series because we are in love with Ty and Zane but the development of the secondary characters (and all of their traits) are what bring the story into the realm of "all-time favorites". Julian's epic Alpha-suaveness, Cameron's vulnerability and Preston's aloof perfection are qualities you want to explore more.<br><br>I've noticed some readers not caring for Cameron but I have to say his character is just one of my favorites. I think it is because he is me. He brings a 'normal human element into this story of 'super-perfect-cool-spy-guys that let's me identify with and allows me "into" the story. I love that!<br>_______________________<br><br><b>The Writing:</b> is quick paced, immediately gripping and doesn't slow down...except where you want it to. The very best thing about this book for me was the amount of dialog. There was plenty of visual orientation, I never felt like I couldn't see what was going on but it was the deep and heartfelt exchanges and the quick, quirky comebacks that just drove this on. So often when I read I get bogged down inside character dialog though and the author is incredibly astute in keeping that from happening. There were glimpses of third-party elements essential to the story that came through perfectly clearly but did not slow the story down. Thank you!<br><br>So again, I say that this book was a gift from Abigail Roux to her readers. Probably in reparation for what she did to them at the end of book 4, but a gift nonetheless.<br><br>I gladly give this book 5 stars and the accolade of, "I can't wait for the next one".<br><br>~~~<br><br><b>Take a look at my Male/Male Romance Book Blog:</b> <br><br><a href="http://www.attentionisarbitrary.blogspot.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379800439i/669513._SX540_.png" width="310" height="133" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>http://www.attentionisarbitrary.blogspot.com </a><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16162536529065595729" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_594435928" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/594435928" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/594435928?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer594435928" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1953418470136611274">The fifth installment of the Cut & Run Series certainly lived up to its name, and then some. That "some" would be Julian Cross, Cameron Jacobs, Preston (forgot his last name), Blake Nichols and yes, even Smith and Wesson made an appearance here. <br/><br/>This book picked up where Divide & Conquer left off, where Zane woke up finding a note and Ty gone. Well, I'm happy to say that all is well in paradise once again for these two. Ty got his head on straight and is in deep cover for another case and Zane w</span>
  <span id="freeText1953418470136611274" style="display:none">The fifth installment of the Cut &amp; Run Series certainly lived up to its name, and then some. That "some" would be Julian Cross, Cameron Jacobs, Preston (forgot his last name), Blake Nichols and yes, even Smith and Wesson made an appearance here. <br /><br />This book picked up where Divide &amp; Conquer left off, where Zane woke up finding a note and Ty gone. Well, I'm happy to say that all is well in paradise once again for these two. Ty got his head on straight and is in deep cover for another case and Zane was sent to back him up. Thank you, Dick! <br /><br />Anyway, Zane wants Ty to grovel. Ha! So cute really. I was smiling the whole the time during their reunion at the airport, all the way to their hotel room where the proper reunion took place. And boy, what a reunion it was! I was thinking maybe they should be apart more in the future just so I can witness another reunion between them. It was that hot! <br /><br />Turns out that our boys are tasked to transport a very important witness and bring that witness back to D.C. The witness is, of course, Julian Cross. Julian was a hostile witness. He wasn't up to cooperating with Ty &amp; Zane. With Cameron in tow, he made Ty &amp; Zane's job hilariously difficult. Yeah, the four of them inside one car and even sharing hotel rooms in between was funny. I found myself laughing out loud many times. Julian stoic and deadpan humor was a match for Ty's snarky one-liner. Haha! I won't list them all here but you can check out my statuses to see what I mean. <br /><br />The whole mystery with who wants Julian killed was a little obvious to me but it was still fun reading about it especially the ending. LoL! But I was a little sad too when Ty &amp; Zane realized that they could never be as free to express their feelings especially since they work together. And when Zane thought that Ty could never introduce him to his family the way Deuce can with his girlfriend, I felt really bad for them. <br /><br />This series just keeps getting better and better, and I can't wait to read more of Ty and Zane! Five down, two more books to go!<br /><br />For more reviews, visit <a href="http://everafterromancebookblog.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Ever After Romance Blog</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1953418470136611274" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1955595193" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17461770155810824909"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*MY BABY TY*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br/><b>
  <u>Re-read: 11.06.2017</u>
</b><br/>Why I started re-reading this one as well is a good question... I think I just wanted more Ty. Because Ty is amazing and I love him so, so much. I still don't like how Julian appeared to be 'better' than Ty, but Ty clearly wins that one; he's simply the best. I also don't get how <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Burs can turn out to be the bad guy late in the book series. I mean, we read his POVs, and he doesn't seem like the bad guy. So it's safe to say that I d</span></span>
  <span id="freeText17461770155810824909" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*MY BABY TY*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <u>Re-read: 11.06.2017</u>
</b><br>Why I started re-reading this one as well is a good question... I think I just wanted more Ty. Because Ty is amazing and I love him so, so much. I still don't like how Julian appeared to be 'better' than Ty, but Ty clearly wins that one; he's simply the best. I also don't get how <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Burs can turn out to be the bad guy late in the book series. I mean, we read his POVs, and he doesn't seem like the bad guy. So it's safe to say that I didn't like that twist. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Overall, I adore and love Ty way too much so the storyline obviously comes second as Ty comes first. I have a feeling that I'll re-read this one again...along with all the others I keep re-reading.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>First read review</u>:</b><br><b>The book was alright</b>, I guess. A bit boring, even with the twists and turns it had. I loved, though, seeing <b>Ty Grady</b> and <b>Zane Garrett</b> more <i>free</i> and more open with each other. It was kinda interesting to see Ty and Zane <b>through someone else's eyes</b>, though I wasn't really interested in Cameron and Julian's relationship, but I liked see how they saw Ty and Zane. Also, I didn't like how the book made me think that Julian was...stronger, more dangerous and more powerful than Ty. In my head, <b>Ty's the most dangerous, the strongest and the most powerful</b>, and I don't like people <i>messing</i> with that. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re not going to kill them, are you?” Cameron asked, shifting uneasily in the seat. “I mean, they’re just doing their jobs.”<br>“Not unless they make me,” Julian said as he looked back at Cameron. “The threat from Grady is negligible, but Garrett will kill both of us if he thinks he’s justified. Remember that before you get too attached to them.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1490780489ra/22343197.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Contemporary Romance (M/M)<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book Five<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Open ending?. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Ty Grady.<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - No.<br><b>Rating</b> - 2.5/3 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_393810112" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/393810112" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/393810112?book_show_action=true">Aug 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer393810112" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2478349399339522524"><b>5 ★★★★★’s</b><br/><br/><b>Pfftt!! Do I even need to say it??!!! OK..I WILL…ANOTHER FUCKING AMAZING BOOK!!!!!!!!</b><br/><br/>It’s getting a little bit more challenging to write good reviews… because I’m starting to sound like a broken record. But I take comfort in knowing that anyone whose read a Cut & Run book totally gets it. And by this point I really don’t need to say much. These boys just freaking <b>ROCK MY WORLD</b>!!!!!!!!!!<br/><br/>Armed & Dangerous is no exception. In fact the stories just keep getting better and better….if that is</span>
  <span id="freeText2478349399339522524" style="display:none"><b>5 ★★★★★’s</b><br><br><b>Pfftt!! Do I even need to say it??!!! OK..I WILL…ANOTHER FUCKING AMAZING BOOK!!!!!!!!</b><br><br>It’s getting a little bit more challenging to write good reviews… because I’m starting to sound like a broken record. But I take comfort in knowing that anyone whose read a Cut &amp; Run book totally gets it. And by this point I really don’t need to say much. These boys just freaking <b>ROCK MY WORLD</b>!!!!!!!!!!<br><br>Armed &amp; Dangerous is no exception. In fact the stories just keep getting better and better….if that is even possible. But then I’m a girl in love, so my opinion may be slightly biased!!!!! <br><br>Just a quick recap…<br><br>This story picks up after <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Ty’s big exit. He’s been off the grid now for only a few days…but Zane’s been feeling the loss deep in his soul, not knowing where Ty’s gone, or why. He doesn’t even know where their relationship stands after that abrupt and secretive exit. Especially after Zane’s big declaration, and Ty’s encounter with Nick.<br><br><b><i>”I told you I loved you, and the next day you were gone.</i></b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>And meanwhile, before Ty can set things right, he gets an unexpected call from Richard Burns, which will require him to complete a job, going dark for an unknown period of time. Ty does move on this order, but not without contacting Zane first. He has been gone now for almost a week,<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ and he knows Zane isn’t going to easily forgive him for his abrupt departure. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And about this …he is absolutely right. He doesn’t give away much to Zane… but he does attempt to ease his fears… and to let him know his feelings haven’t changed.<br><br>Meanwhile, Zane gets a call from Richard Burns as well….also sending him out on a special assignment. No details, just a plane ticket to Chicago, and a hint that he will be backing up another agent off the grid. But it doesn’t take him long to find out, once he arrives that indeed, he will be taking Ty’s back on this case. And it’s no secret that he is torn from being completely thrilled at seeing his partner again, and wanting to beat the life out of him at the same time. <br><br>Well…long story short…they kiss and make up, but quickly, because the case they’ re working is exploding fast. They must quickly locate and take into custody a CIA wet works operator that is the last living evidence to clear a higher up in the agency who is being framed for multiple crimes, such as misappropriation of funds, and multiple ordered assassinations. <br><br>Julian Cross was their target. He was also a highly trained and a very apt assassin. He was also gay. In fact they locate him through his lover Cameron Jacobs. Cross was an Irishman, and very much-resembled Zane in appearance, and in a similar way was a very smooth operator. His lover, Cameron, was a waiter at a local restaurant that he frequented. But Cameron was a no-nonsense guy…an innocent. He knew Julian was into something dangerous rather than just the antique business he admitted to. But he figured the less he knew, the better. He knew that Julian loved him, and would protect him, and that was all he decided to care about.<br><br>Well put these four guys together on a trip from Chicago to DC and let me tell you it was a trip to remember. Emotions were high; egos were flaring, and not without blood shed. Cross was determined to escape. And let’s just say that Ty made it his life mission to keep that from happening. What a wild ride. It was like Midnight Run on steroids!!! Lots of verbal sparring, creative usage of hand-cuffs, and four-letter-words!!! And not to mention inventive traveling games….<br><br><b>
  <i>”Glock, paper, scissors, I win.”,</i>
</b>- Ty<br><br>So funny, so intense, and between Ty and Cameron the one-liners are never ending and absolutely priceless!!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>”I don’t think I’ve ever been gayer than I am right now.”</i>
</b><br><br> ***<br><br><b>
  <i>”You need a Valium or something,” Cameron said under his breath as he tried to hurry enough that Ty wouldn’t drag him.<br>	“Yes, I do. I should also be given a cigarette after what that TSA agent did to me,” Ty snapped.</i>
</b><br><br> ***<br><br><b>
  <i>”You need a little love in your life,” Cameron told him.<br>Ty narrowed his eyes but had nothing sarcastic to say to that.<br>“Really, “ Cameron said, just to get in a dig of his own for being dragged around. “It did wonders for Julian’s attitude.”</i>
</b><br><br> ***<br><br><b>
  <i>”If we start freezing, we’re eating Cameron first,” Ty grunted before unbuckling his seatbelt and climbing out of the car.</i>
</b><br><br>Just so you know…Cameron was just adorable. So innocent, such a romantic. Ty and Zane both felt guilty about his involvement in the case, but his presence was very important nonetheless. His dialogue was just fantastic, warm and heartfelt… naïve, but at the same time practical. There was no doubt, that by the end, Ty and Zane both developed both a respect and fondness for both Julian and Cameron. I expect more involvement from these two in future books. <br><br><b>
  <i>”I hate it when mother and father fight,” Julian said under his breath.<br>“Shut up,” Ty snapped at him, then turned on Zane, who stood to meet him. “Sit down, take a bubble bath or something, I need to take a walk.”<br>“Goddammit!” Zane lashed out without warning….”Loving you is going to make me fucking insane! I said NO, and I mean it!”</i>
</b><br><br>Oops…busted…<b>
  <i>”I did not see that coming,”</i>
</b> Julian said to Cameron under his breath.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You totally just outed us to the criminals."</i>
</b><br><br>Then there was Nick. Called back into play to help out in a time of need. But was also called out by Zane, wanting answers. What an enlightening moment that was too!!!!! But in the end, Zane got what he needed in order to move forward. But I don’t think that’s the last we’ll hear from Nick O’Flaherty.<br><br>And lastly, there’s Ty and Zane. Wow…such tension, newfound trust, and feelings of uninhibited love!!!! But with that will come the desire to expose their relationship and finally be able to be together…live together. But this will not accepted by their employer…no exceptions. So where they go from here will be interesting. <br><br>And I can’t wait to get to the next chapter in their life… Stars &amp; Stripes, here I come!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>"Ready to go fuck with the Agency?" A cold ball of determination settled in the pit of Ty's stomach. He took the handcuffs and grinned wolfishly. "They messed with the wrong Feebs this time."</i>
</b><br><br>This story was much more involved than I could have imagined. Very suspenseful. Unpredictable. Riveting. Hilarious. Sexy. Romantic. Fan-fucking-tastic!!!! <br><br><b>
  <i>"This is stupid," Cameron muttered as he rubbed his hands over his face. "I can't believe this is real life."</i>
</b> <br><br>Here are my pics…<br><br><b>Special Agent Ty Grady <br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/channing_tatum_white_house_down1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910753i/3190764._SX540_.jpg" alt="Channing Tatum photo channing_tatum_white_house_down1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Special Agent Zane Garrett</b>(with the ferret's nest!)<br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/marcodapper.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910753i/3190765.jpg" alt="Marco Dapper photo marcodapper.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Julian Cross<br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/JustinClynes3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910753i/3190768.jpg" alt="Justin Clynes photo JustinClynes3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Cameron Jacobs</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/CalebLane7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_267647940" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/267647940" />
    <a title="Jess Candela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6159912-jess-candela"><img alt="Jess Candela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370106927p2/6159912.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/267647940?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jess Candela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jess Candela" href="/user/show/6159912-jess-candela">Jess Candela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6159912-jess-candela?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6159912-jess-candela?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6159912-jess-candela?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer267647940" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1802529275409274363">I very carefully stayed off Goodreads from the moment I got the book until I finished reading it. I look forward to having my opinion in rereads influenced by what others think but for the first read I wanted to have my own reactions in isolation.<br/><br/>I think the core of this book was about trust. Ty and Zane learning to trust each other emotionally. Or, maybe, not learning so much as finally just taking a deep breath and taking the plunge. The learning curve occurred in the earlier books. And, of co</span>
  <span id="freeText1802529275409274363" style="display:none">I very carefully stayed off Goodreads from the moment I got the book until I finished reading it. I look forward to having my opinion in rereads influenced by what others think but for the first read I wanted to have my own reactions in isolation.<br /><br />I think the core of this book was about trust. Ty and Zane learning to trust each other emotionally. Or, maybe, not learning so much as finally just taking a deep breath and taking the plunge. The learning curve occurred in the earlier books. And, of course, they've already developed complete trust in the other having his back in any dangerous situation.<br /><br />Trust between old war buddies: Burns and Jonas, and of course, Ty and Nick. When Jonas comes to Burns at the beginning of the story with an outrageous story and no proof, Burns trusts him implicitly because of their history together. Later in the book we learn more about Ty and Nick's history, and better understand the trust between them and why it's an unshakeable bond. There are enough parallels to help make clear, I think, the depth of the trust between Burns and Jonas.<br /><br />When Zane finally talks to Nick, we see a trust develop between them. A trust that they both love Ty, both want what is best for him, and both agree that is clearly Zane. With that understanding and trust, the door opens for Zane and Nick to become real friends, too. I was never a Nick-hater after the last book, feeling sympathetic to his circumstances. I was glad to see my trust borne out in this book.<br /><br />There's also the trust between Julian and Cameron. Cam trusts Julian to take care of him, trusts that if Julian says all is well (or will be)... he knows Julian well enough to know that might not be true in the moment, that Julian may just be trying to protect him and keep him from worrying. But he has enough trust in Julian's intent and ability to care for him that even when he knows Julian is lying, he can still trust him. And Julian trusts Cameron to assist in that protection, to not be a liability. Eventually, Ty and Zane build a trust with Julian that they're all on the same side: wanting the four of them to make it to DC alive.<br /><br />There's also Ty's trust in Burns, complete after growing up with the man as his father's best friend and honed over years of working for him. Zane also trusts Burns, based on his own history working for him. So even when circumstances might suggest that Burns could be betraying them, and possibly trying to kill them, they ignore the evidence based on the trust of years.<br /><br />One thing I didn't understand <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[was why Preston wasn't following the foursome from the very beginning, to assist Julian in escaping from Ty and Zane. I know they said Preston would watch the cats, but based on their history I really expected Preston to make some sort of arrangements and then be hot on their heels. Also, I kind of expected Ty to have more reaction to Jonas' betrayal, but perhaps we'll see more of that in the next book. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Miscellaneous thoughts:<br /><br />At the risk of psychoanalyzing without a license, but knowing some of the circumstances about how this went from being a co-authored series to a solo one, I imagine trust and betrayal of trust was very much on Abigail's mind as she wrote it. I know a lot of the plot changed when it became a solo work, and I wonder if the trust theme is new or was part of the original plot.<br /><br />This book answered most of the open questions from the last one, about why Ty left (and where he went), about Nick, about that darn necklace from F&amp;C.<br /><br />It was great spending more time with Deuce, and seeing what he's up to. It was also fun to visit his home and learn a bit more about him that way.<br /><br />I loved the tenderness Ty and Zane finally allowed themselves to display. And how they really started to settle into becoming a true couple. I think they had reached the point of (to put it crudely) shit or get off the pot, when romantic relationships either end or deepen into something lasting. I had assumed it would last, given there are several more books in the series, but it's one thing to assume and another thing to witness it happening so beautifully. I loved seeing them really talk and open up to each other finally.<br /><br />And, needless to say, I'm delighted that the wait for the next book is only a couple of months. Of course, even that is still too much! But maybe not, as I think it's good to have some time to digest between the books. So the time between this release and the next one is probably just about perfect. Dare I hope there will be a similar spacing between books 6 and 7?</span>
  <a data-text-id="1802529275409274363" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time">Heather K (dentist in my spare time)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=loved-it">loved-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=sex-sex-and-more-sex">sex-sex-and-more-sex</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=favorites-2012">favorites-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=great-chemistry">great-chemistry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=police-or-military">police-or-military</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer447609511" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer755685702328614889">Phew! A return back to awesomeness from my favorite Ty and Zane. I love their openness in this book. Such a nice change of pace! I also loved how they played off of Cam and Julian. All and all it was sweet, exciting, and very enjoyable. I have a lot of time and energy invested in Ty and Zane's relationship so I'm just excited to be along for the very bumpy ride! </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_605050726" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/605050726" />
    <a title="Ingie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie"><img alt="Ingie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477339772p2/15589375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/605050726?book_show_action=true">May 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ingie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ingie" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie">Ingie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781613725122" href="/book/show/15896656-armed-dangerous">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-m-novels">romance-m-m-novels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=books-i-read-2013">books-i-read-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=series-part-two-three-etc">series-part-two-three-etc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer605050726" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18292956423915642462"><b>Book #5 and 4,5 Big Stars for another enjoying and exciting story with my favorite FBI agents; Ty & Zane<br/><br/>...and two old acquaintances, the lovely Julian & Cameron, from another wonderful M/M romance by this author.</b><br/><br/>This spring I read my first romance book about <b>"boys who loves boys"</b>. Now I'm really stuck in this genre (I want to meet more lovely gay guys) and what isn't better to satisfy my new needs, than a new book about this two gorgeous boys, Ty Grady and Zane Garrett. The fifth one for me and</span>
  <span id="freeText18292956423915642462" style="display:none"><b>Book #5 and 4,5 Big Stars for another enjoying and exciting story with my favorite FBI agents; Ty &amp; Zane<br><br>...and two old acquaintances, the lovely Julian &amp; Cameron, from another wonderful M/M romance by this author.</b><br><br>This spring I read my first romance book about <b>"boys who loves boys"</b>. Now I'm really stuck in this genre (I want to meet more lovely gay guys) and what isn't better to satisfy my new needs, than a new book about this two gorgeous boys, Ty Grady and Zane Garrett. The fifth one for me and with a shiver of delight, I start to read.<br><blockquote>"Does it make you feel better to know that I missed the hell out of you?" Ty whispered, lips moving against Zane's. "And I hope your still just a little angry when get back to my hotel."<br>Zane let out a shuttering breath, "It'll be more than just a little."<br>Ty hummed, the sound deep and anticipatory. It was almost a purr. "Promise?"</blockquote><br><b>As I said before are these "Cut &amp; Run" novels</b> perhaps the best form of an continuous romance series. It's so simple - it's just some looks, acts, feelings and sweet, tender words - that make Ty and Zane's romantic adventure to a slow build-up unforgettable story about big male LOVE. As a friend use to say in her reviews of books with grand love; an <b>epic story</b>.<br><br><b>In this fifth book are these both FBI agents</b> in Chicago on FBI director Richard Burn's secret orders. Ty and Zane (so passionately in love) have been assigned to, with as little fuss as possible, bring a former hit man, south to Washington and the FBI headquarters. The man in question, <b>Julian Cross</b> is witness to an internal scandal at CSI with powerful men involved. <br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Pics/Hotties/4b74baef_zps9a9285e7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419907i/832800.jpg" alt=" photo 4b74baef_zps9a9285e7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <br>
  <i>Four of my favorite guys in the same book - <br>what an opportunity!</i>
</blockquote><br>We know, the tough and scary Julian and his sweet and a little more delicate boyfriend, <b>Cameron Jacobs</b>, since the excellent novel, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6782412.Warrior_s_Cross" title="Warrior's Cross by Abigail Roux" rel="nofollow noopener">Warrior's Cross</a>. These two so enamored "love pigeons", is of course not entirely willing to do whatever, primarily Ty, so assertive commands. Three alpha males meet and there will be many witty and funny word-battles and it's "pushing and pinching" between these tough, bossy "cocks". <i>Who has the real power in the henhouse?</i> Of course it will be a great adventure of their, originally intended as simple, travel south with a lot of smart enemies in their heels.<br><blockquote>“What? It’s not my blood!”<br>“Let me see it,” Julian demanded, and a moment later there were sounds of a scuffle from the back seat.<br>“I am AB positive and this is distinctly type O blood!” Ty finally shouted at him. “Look at the little Os!” </blockquote><br><b>Like in book 1-4 happens</b> a number of nasty incidents around these two agents and I'm on the edge all the time. Whether some suspense, mysteries and FBI work, this is mainly novels about love. Male beautiful love with so nicely and tender descrieb love scenes. It's hot and steamy but always sweet. <br><br><b>Ty and Zane takes some more considerable</b> progress in their relationship in this fifth novel. It's these elements - the boys fine, a little tentative, declarations of love and more - as I after all love so much with these books. <br><blockquote>Ty slid his hand down Zane's arm and linked their fingers again. "That I can hold your hand without worrying about being reconized.” <br>~ ~ ~ ~<br>“I don't think I've ever been gayer than I am right now.”</blockquote><br><b>I'd very much like to get a little more</b> about how Julian's and Cameron's relationship has evolved (it has been a year since we were meeting them last), but it is perhaps difficult for the author to get into this too well in this book. But do you know these other two wedges a little more, do not miss to read their own book (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/597664437" rel="nofollow noopener">5 stars from me</a>).<br><blockquote>“Cameron found himself smiling as he thought about the two tough, acerbic FBI agents. "It's so cute. They're in love."<br>"It's like watching two kittens fight with machetes," Julian muttered.”<br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Quotes/quote-2_zps60098170.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418871i/829780.jpg" alt=" photo quote-2_zps60098170.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br><b>As I'm spoiled with</b> - it's a lot of good dialogue, funny statements, witty replys, loving words - in this book as well. It's always quick shifts between full action, wonderful artful dialogue and tender, VERY hot love scenes.<br><br>If you, who are reading my reviews, havn't already understand that I'm full of admiration and <b>in deep love</b> in Ty and Zane, the ”Cut &amp; Run" series and this talented author miss Roux , I say it out LOUD one more time: <i>
  <b>I love these books!</b>
</i> <br><br>I look forward to read the next installment in this wonderful series. <br><br><b>I LIKE - it's a great series!</b><br><br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br><i>The four previous books in the series that I read: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/531276012" rel="nofollow noopener">my review Cut &amp; Run #1</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/592712646" rel="nofollow noopener">my review Sticks &amp; Stones #2</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/603649594" rel="nofollow noopener">my review Fish &amp; Chips #3</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/603649986" rel="nofollow noopener">my review Divide &amp; Conquer #4</a></i> <br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Quotes/AnimatedWords_zps206e0229.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408914ra/800310.gif" alt=" photo AnimatedWords_zps206e0229.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="18292956423915642462" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_489258776" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489258776" />
    <a title="Lisazj1" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5816343-lisazj1"><img alt="Lisazj1" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1337769434p2/5816343.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/489258776?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisazj1" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisazj1" href="/user/show/5816343-lisazj1">Lisazj1</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781613725122" href="/book/show/15896656-armed-dangerous">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=real-book-shelf">real-book-shelf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=oh-my-heart">oh-my-heart</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=loved-loved-loved">loved-loved-loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=omg-hoooottttttt">omg-hoooottttttt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=kickin-butt">kickin-butt</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer489258776" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer197214003992423736">*3rd read 2020*<br/><br/>My God, they melt me like butter on a hot stove, and I regret <i>nothing</i>. It just isn't possible to love fictional characters more. ❤️❤️❤️<br/><br/>*Re-read 2018*<br/><br/>SO. MUCH. SWOON. So much! *sigh* <br/><br/>*1st read 2012*<br/><br/>I about ripped the cover on this book, I couldn't get it open fast enough after the ending of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12384681.Divide___Conquer__Cut___Run___4_' title='Divide & Conquer (Cut & Run, #4) by Abigail Roux' rel='nofollow noopener'>Divide & Conquer</a>. Thank goodness I didn't have to wait for my answers, at all. That's one thing among many that I love about this series. There's angst, quite a bit of it, in fact. But it isn't </span>
  <span id="freeText197214003992423736" style="display:none">*3rd read 2020*<br /><br />My God, they melt me like butter on a hot stove, and I regret <i>nothing</i>. It just isn't possible to love fictional characters more. ❤️❤️❤️<br /><br />*Re-read 2018*<br /><br />SO. MUCH. SWOON. So much! *sigh* <br /><br />*1st read 2012*<br /><br />I about ripped the cover on this book, I couldn't get it open fast enough after the ending of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12384681.Divide___Conquer__Cut___Run___4_" title="Divide &amp; Conquer (Cut &amp; Run, #4) by Abigail Roux" rel="nofollow noopener">Divide &amp; Conquer</a>. Thank goodness I didn't have to wait for my answers, at all. That's one thing among many that I love about this series. There's angst, quite a bit of it, in fact. But it isn't the main focus of the story and usually, the worst things are resolved without allowing it be be dragged out interminably. *huffs*. Though resolved, like Zane, I was <i>STILL</i> a bit pissed off. *rolls eyes* Men! I swear to God...so stupid sometimes.<br /><br />So, Ty gets sent on another black ops job (sort of) by Director Burns *at the WORST possible time* *huffs again*. The difference is, Zane ends up being with him on this one. From the beginning, I felt the shift in them, and to be honest, it kind of freaked me out. Everything changed once <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Zane finally was able to say "I love you" back to Ty <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. But, especially being who &amp; how Ty &amp; Zane are, I guess that would have to change the way they interacted. But as I read on, the change in their dynamic was, though I wouldn't have believed it, even better than before. I still get the well written action and suspense and things going BOOM, but I also get to be a swoony-sighing girl more too. Win/win for me.<br /><br />The guys have been sent to retrieve a CIA wetworks operative named Julian Cross. Taking Cross on his own is risky enough, but he refuses to go peacefully *coughbullshitcough* without his boyfriend Cameron Jacobs, who has gotten caught in the middle of all this. Julian Cross is a dangerous man. He's also determined to be the broken cog in the wheel of Ty &amp; Zane's operation, and some of the things that he does to slow them down while he plots to escape had me laughing my ass off! Cameron was just a sweet, everyday kind of guy who happened to be in love with a guy who was anything but the everyday type. But I loved Cameron being unable to turn off what he thought was right, even when it was Ty &amp; Zane he had to consider.<br /><br />The worst thing about this operation was that everything everyone, including Director Burns, thought they knew was wrong. When it became clear (to the reader, anyway) what was really going on, I was afraid for the boys, because I didn't see any way it could end well. <br /><br />As for what's between Ty &amp; Zane now...reading the things they say and do to each other never, ever fails to play with my heart. But now, there's more hope than hurt. They aren't hiding from each other or themselves anymore. And omg, it's so tender and sweet and LOL funny, as well as sexy and fucking hot that I wish I would never run out of Ty &amp; Zane stories to read. Write faster, Abigail Roux!! :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="197214003992423736" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('dYoXz6bU2wPW6WPGJ0KEsTSc2Cf4yx5txshn5AhSfyv7HPznLNI9SQjgBvcJLrLOf7Eu1dBht2KK7NDE0b+Frg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ST358+n56f08i5inavO9sp7ZsW6+33EPS/9UZz2b2vXHqxLbY/8Pt+KC/ZZEn4vN1fRHnJZ12AAH2+NH5HYgcA==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer14176858660372084228">Abigail Roux was born and raised in North Carolina. A past volleyball star who specializes in sarcasm and painful historical accuracy, she currently spends her time coaching high school volleyball and investigating the mysteries of single motherhood. Any spare time is spent living and dying with every Atlanta Braves and Carolina Panthers game of the year. Abigail has a daughter, Little Roux, who i</span>
  <span id="freeText14176858660372084228" style="display:none">Abigail Roux was born and raised in North Carolina. A past volleyball star who specializes in sarcasm and painful historical accuracy, she currently spends her time coaching high school volleyball and investigating the mysteries of single motherhood. Any spare time is spent living and dying with every Atlanta Braves and Carolina Panthers game of the year. Abigail has a daughter, Little Roux, who is the light of her life, a boxer, four rescued cats who play an ongoing live-action variation of 'Call of Duty' throughout the house, a certifiable extended family down the road, and a cast of thousands in her head.</span>

Two out of three.”<br />Ty rolled his eyes and held out his fist, apparently willing to play. Julian hit his palm three times, and Ty kept time with his fist in the air. But when Julian threw a paper, Ty reached into his jacket with his other hand and pulled his gun, aiming it at Julian.<br />“Ty!” Zane said in exasperation from the front seat.<br />“Glock, paper, scissors. I win.”<br />“You are an ass,” Julian muttered.&rdquo;</span>
